install.packages("igraph")
install.packages("ggmap")
install.packages("geosphere")
install.packages("rgeos")
library(igraph)
library(ggplot2)
library(ggmap)
library(plyr)
library(maps)
library(rgeos)
library(ggmap)
library(geosphere)
library(dplyr)

df=read.csv("routes_main.csv")

rm(list = ls())

fortify.SpatialLinesDataFrame = function(model, data, ...){
  ldply(model@lines, fortify)
}

routes = gcIntermediate(df[,c('lon1', 'lat1')], df[,c('lon2', 'lat2')], 200, breakAtDateLine = FALSE, addStartEnd = TRUE, sp=TRUE)

fortifiedroutes = fortify.SpatialLinesDataFrame(routes)

worldmap = map_data ("world")

wrld=c(geom_polygon(aes(long,lat,group=group), size = 0.1, colour= "#090D2A",
                     fill="#090D2A", alpha=0.8, data=worldmap))

ggplot()+ wrld +geom_line(aes(long,lat,group=id), alpha = 0.3, size=0.01, data= fortifiedroutes) +
  theme(panel.background = element_rect(fill="white",colour="white"), panel.grid.major = element_blank(), panel.grid.minor = element_blank()) +
  theme(legend.position = c(0,0.4),
        legend.justification = c(0,1),
        legend.background = element_rect(colour = NA, fill = NA),
        legend.key = element_rect(colour = NA, fill = NA, size = 10),
        )

net <- graph_from_data_frame(df, directed = FALSE)
net

clique.number(net)
largest.cliques(net)

wc=walktrap.community(net)
wc
sort(membership(wc))
modularity(wc)

lec = leading.eigenvector.community(net)
sort(membership(lec))
modularity(lec)

degree=degree(net)
degree
max(degree)
V(net)$name[degree(net)==max(degree(net))]
degree(net)
sort(degree(net),decreasing=FALSE)

#Obtain Betweenness Score
nodes <- read.csv("NODES.csv")
edges <- read.csv("Edges.csv")
net <- graph_from_data_frame(edges, directed = TRUE, vertices = nodes)
vertex_betweenness <- sort((betweenness(net)),decreasing=TRUE)[1:10]
vertex_betweenness

#Analysis of Betweenness Scores
airport_stats <- read.csv("Airport Statistics.csv")

#With Airport Passenger Numbers
ggplot(data = airport_stats, mapping = aes(x = Betweenness.Score, y = Passenger.Movement..2018.)) + labs(title="Betweenness Score & Airport Passenger Numbers Analysis",x="Betweenness Score", y = "Passenger Numbers (2018)") + geom_text(aes(label = airport_stats$IATA.Code, colour = airport_stats$IATA.Code)) + geom_smooth(se = FALSE, method = "lm") + scale_fill_manual(values = alpha(c("#000000", "#FF5733")))
#With Cargo in Tonnes
ggplot(data = airport_stats, mapping = aes(x = Betweenness.Score, y = Cargo.Movement.in.Tonnes..2018.)) + labs(title="Betweenness Score & Cargo Load Analysis",x="Betweenness Score", y = "Cargo in Tonnes (2018)") + geom_text(aes(label = airport_stats$IATA.Code, colour = airport_stats$IATA.Code)) + geom_smooth(se = FALSE, method = "lm") + scale_fill_manual(values = alpha(c("#000000", "#FF5733")))

#With Airport Passenger Numbers
ggplot(data = airport_stats, mapping = aes(x = Betweenness.Score, y = Passenger.Movement..2018.)) + labs(title="Betweenness Score & Airport Passenger Numbers Analysis",x="Betweenness Score", y = "Passenger Numbers (2018)") + geom_text(label = airport_stats$IATA.Code) + geom_smooth(se = FALSE, method = "lm")
#With Cargo in Tonnes
ggplot(data = airport_stats, mapping = aes(x = Betweenness.Score, y = Cargo.Movement.in.Tonnes..2018.)) + labs(title="Betweenness Score & Cargo Load Analysis",x="Betweenness Score", y = "Cargo in Tonnes (2018)") + geom_text(label = airport_stats$IATA.Code) + geom_smooth(se = FALSE, method = "lm")

##### Pre-processing and Graph (directed) creation for Network Analysis #####


# Edges
edge_routes <- read.csv("routes.csv", encoding = "UTF-8", stringsAsFactors = FALSE)
edge_routes <- edge_routes[, c(4, 6, 3, 5, 1, 2, 7, 8, 9)]
colnames(edge_routes)[1:2] <- c("Source", "Target")

# Nodes
nodes_airports <- read.csv("airports_extended.csv", header=FALSE, encoding = "UTF-8", stringsAsFactors = FALSE)
names(nodes_airports) = c("Id", "Label", "City", "Country", "IATA", "ICAO", "Latitude", "Longtitude", "Altitude", "Timezone", "DST", "TZ_Timezone", "Type", "Source")

# Correcting country names in preparation for EDA
nodes_airports[nodes_airports$Country=="United States","Country"]<-"USA"
nodes_airports[nodes_airports$Country=="United Kingdom","Country"]<-"UK"
nodes_airports[nodes_airports$Country=="Cote d\'Ivoire","Country"]<-"Ivory Coast"
nodes_airports[nodes_airports$Country=="Congo (Kinshasa)","Country"]<-"Democratic Republic of the Congo"
nodes_airports[nodes_airports$Country=="Congo (Brazzaville)","Country"]<-"Republic of Congo"




# Pre-processing
# Drop Source and Target = \\N i.e. NULL values
edge_routes <- edge_routes[!(edge_routes$Source=="\\N" | edge_routes$Target== "\\N"),]
edge_routes$Source <- factor(edge_routes$Source)
edge_routes$Target <- factor(edge_routes$Target)

# Keep airport information of only those found in routes (edges)
u <- factor(union(edge_routes$Source, edge_routes$Target))
nodes_airports <- nodes_airports[(nodes_airports$Id %in% u), ]

g <- graph_from_data_frame(d = edge_routes, vertices = nodes_airports, directed=TRUE)

# Simpliied version
gS <- g
E(gS)$weight <- 1
gS <- simplify(gS, edge.attr.comb = list(weight="sum"))


##### Network Statistics #####
# Centrality (Degree, Closeness, Betweenness, eigen)#
# PageRank #
# Mean Path Length  #
# Network Diameter #
# Clustering Coefficient #

### Network Summary Stats ###

print("Directed Network Summary Stats:")

# Nodes and edges
paste0("Number of nodes: ", vcount(g))
paste0("Number of edges: ", ecount(g))

# Degree
paste0("Average total degree: ", mean(degree(g, mode="total")))
paste0("Average in-degree/out-degree: ", mean(degree(g, mode="in")))

# Mean path length
paste0("Mean path length: ", mean_distance(g))

# Network Diameter
paste0("Network Diameter: ", diameter(g))

# Global Clustering Coefficient
paste0("Global Clustering Coefficient: ", transitivity(g))


# Node-based statistics
g_dC <- summary(centr_degree(g)$res)
g_cC <- summary(centr_clo(g)$res)
g_bC_vert <- summary(centr_betw(g)$res)
g_bC_edge <- summary(edge_betweenness(g))
g_eC <- summary(centr_eigen(g)$res)
g_PR <- summary(page_rank(g)$vector)
g_cl <- summary(transitivity(g, type="local"))[1:6]

g_summary <- data.frame(rbind(g_dC, g_cC, g_bC_vert, g_bC_edge, g_eC, g_PR, g_cl))
g_summary





### Distribution curves ###
# Degree distribution #
# Clustering coefficient distribution #
# Hub + Authority + PageRank Distribution #

# Degree Distribution #
degcount <- data.frame(degK = degree(g)) %>% 
  group_by(degK) %>% 
  summarise(num = n(), pK = num/3300)

# Raw plot
degcount %>% ggplot() +
  geom_point(aes(x=degK, y=pK), size=4, color="#451077", pch=1) +
  theme(axis.text = element_text(size=14), axis.title = element_text(size=14), plot.title = element_text(size=24)) +
  labs(title="Degree Distribution", x="k", y="P(k)")

# Raw plot (zoomed in)
degcount %>% ggplot() +
  geom_point(aes(x=degK, y=pK), size=4, color="#451077", pch=1) +
  theme(axis.text = element_text(size=14), axis.title = element_text(size=14), plot.title = element_text(size=24)) +
  labs(title="Degree Distribution", x="k", y="P(k)") +
  coord_cartesian(xlim=c(0,100), ylim=c(0,0.1))

# Log-log plot
degcount %>% ggplot() +
  geom_point(aes(x=degK, y=pK), size=4, color="#451077", pch=1) +
  theme(axis.text = element_text(size=14), axis.title = element_text(size=14), plot.title = element_text(size=24)) +
  labs(title="Degree Distribution (log-log)", x="k", y="P(k)") +
  scale_x_log10() + scale_y_log10()

# In-degree distribution
degINcount <- data.frame(degK = degree(g, mode="in")) %>% 
  group_by(degK) %>% 
  summarise(num = n(), pK = num/3300)

# Raw plot
degINcount %>% ggplot() +
  geom_point(aes(x=degK, y=pK), size=4, color="#451077") +
  theme(axis.text = element_text(size=14), axis.title = element_text(size=14), plot.title = element_text(size=24)) +
  labs(title="In-Degree Distribution", x="k", y="P(k)")

# Log=log plot
degINcount %>% ggplot() +
  geom_point(aes(x=degK, y=pK), size=4, color="#451077") +
  theme(axis.text = element_text(size=14), axis.title = element_text(size=14), plot.title = element_text(size=24)) +
  labs(title="In-Degree Distribution (log-log)", x="k", y="P(k)") + 
  scale_x_log10() + scale_y_log10()

# Out-degree distribution
degOUTcount <- data.frame(degK = degree(g, mode="out")) %>% 
  group_by(degK) %>% 
  summarise(num = n(), pK = num/3300)

degOUTcount %>% ggplot() +
  geom_point(aes(x=degK, y=pK), size=4, color="#451077", pch=1) +
  theme(axis.text = element_text(size=14), axis.title = element_text(size=14), plot.title = element_text(size=24)) +
  labs(title="Degree Distribution", x="k", y="P(k)")

ggplot() +
  geom_point(data=degINcount, aes(x=degK, y=pK), size=4, color="#451077", pch=1) +
  geom_point(data=degOUTcount, aes(x=degK, y=pK), size=4, color="orange", pch=1) +
  theme(axis.text = element_text(size=14), axis.title = element_text(size=14), plot.title = element_text(size=24)) +
  labs(title="Degree Distribution", x="k", y="P(k)") +
  scale_x_log10() + scale_y_log10()



### Clustering coefficient distribution
# Find clustering coefficient of each airport/node
clcoeff <- transitivity(g, type="local")

# Find degree of each node
deg <- degree(g)

# Generate a table which relates clustering coefficient distribution  C(k) with degree k
cldist <- cbind(data.frame(deg), clcoeff)
cldist <- cldist %>% 
  group_by(deg) %>% 
  summarize(Ck = mean(clcoeff))

cldist <- cldist[-1,]

# Raw plot
cldist %>% ggplot() +
  geom_point(aes(x=deg, y=Ck), size=3, color="#756bb1") +
  theme(axis.text = element_text(size=14), axis.title = element_text(size=14), plot.title = element_text(size=24)) +
  labs(title="Clustering Coefficient Distribution", x="k", y="C(k)")


# Log-Log plot
cldist %>% ggplot() +
  geom_point(aes(x=deg, y=Ck), size=3, color="#756bb1") +
  theme(axis.text = element_text(size=14), axis.title = element_text(size=14), plot.title = element_text(size=24)) +
  labs(title="Clustering Coefficient Distribution (log-log)", x="k", y="C(k)") +
  scale_x_log10() + scale_y_log10()


### Hub + Authority 


# Authority
g_aut <- table(authority_score(g)$vector)
plot(g_aut, yaxt="none", xaxt="none", type ="p", xlab="Authority Score", ylab="Frequency", main="Authority Score Distribution")
axis(2, seq(0, 42, 10),las=2)
axis(1, seq(0, 1, 0.2))

# Hub
g_hub <- table(hub_score(g)$vector)
plot(g_hub, yaxt="none", xaxt="none", type ="p", xlab="Hub Score", ylab="Frequency", main="Hub Score Distribution")
axis(2, seq(0, 82, 20),las=2)
axis(1, seq(0, 1, 0.2))

    "out_j = routes_clean.groupby(['OrgIATA']).size().reset_index()\n",

    "# Page Rank evaluation:\n",
    "n = len(vertices)\n",
    "n"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 53,
   "metadata": {},
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# Time for computing the Page Rank Algorithm\n",
    "start_time = time.time()"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 54,
   "metadata": {},
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "#This function computes the Page Rank Algorithm\n",
    "\n",
    "def page_rank(n, airports_i, deadEnds_idx, no_input_idx ):\n",
    "    ite = 0\n",
    "    n = n\n",
    "    p = np.ones(n)/n\n",
    "    l = 0.85\n",
    "    comp = (1-l)/n\n",
    "    while ite < 100:\n",
    "        print(ite)\n",
    "        q = np.zeros(n)\n",
    "        p2 = p[deadEnds_idx]\n",
    "        add = p2/n\n",
    "        sum_de = sum(add)\n",
    "        default = (l * sum_de) + comp\n",
    "        q[no_input_idx] = default\n",
    "        for index, row in airports_i.iterrows():\n",
    "            w_ji = row.Weight\n",
    "            out_j = row.Out_j\n",
    "            p_j = p[row.OrgIATA]\n",
    "            sum_ji = p_j*w_ji\n",
    "            sum_ji = sum_ji/out_j\n",
    "            sum_ji = sum(sum_ji) + sum_de\n",
    "            q[row.DstIDX] = (l * sum_ji) + comp\n",
    "        if np.allclose(p, q, rtol=1e-4, atol=1e-4):\n",
    "            break\n",
    "        else:\n",
    "            p = q\n",
    "            ite += 1\n",
    "    return p"
   ]
  },
  {

    "# Page Rank Computation\n",
    "pr = page_rank(n, airports_i, deadEnds_idx, no_input_idx)\n",
    "print(\"--- %s seconds ---\" % (time.time() - start_time))\n",
    "# Get the total sum of P\n",
    "print(sum(pr))"
   ]

#Network Graph in Python#
import networkx as nx
import itertools
import copy
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import warnings
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')

data=pd.read_csv(r'C:\Users\user\Desktop\Edges - Copy.csv')

FG=nx.from_pandas_edgelist(data, source='Source', target='Target', create_using=nx.DiGraph())
FG.nodes()
FG.edges()

nx.draw(FG, with_labels=True)
color_map = {1:'#f09494', 2:'#eebcbc', 3:'#72bbd0', 4:'#91f0a1', 5:'#629fff', 6:'#bcc2f2',  
             7:'#eebcbc', 8:'#f1f0c0', 9:'#d2ffe7', 10:'#caf3a6', 11:'#ffdf55', 12:'#ef77aa', 
             13:'#d6dcff', 14:'#d2f5f0'} 
nx.draw(FG, pos=nx.spring_layout(FG, k=0.8, iterations=50), **options)
ax = plt.gca()
ax.collections[0].set_edgecolor("#555555") 
plt.show()
